hold a conference call on August&#160;14, 2023 at 4:30 p.m.&#160;EDT to discuss these results and the business update.</p>

the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section,
nor shall it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except
as expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing.</p>

<P STYLE="margin: 0; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0; font-size: 10pt"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0; font-size: 10pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>The Metals Company
Provides Second Quarter 2023 <BR>
Corporate Update and Commentary on <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">~$27</FONT> Million Capital Raise at $2.00<BR>
Per Share with Potential Upsizing to $<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">38 </FONT>Million</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">NEW YORK, August 14, 2023 &mdash; TMC
the metals company Inc. (Nasdaq: TMC) (&ldquo;TMC&rdquo; or &ldquo;the Company&rdquo;), an explorer of lower-impact battery metals from
seafloor polymetallic nodules, today provided a corporate update and financial results for the second quarter ending June 30, 2023.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>Q2 2023 Financial Highlights</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 20px"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 20px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Net
                                            loss of $14.1 million and per share <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">amount of $0.05
                                            </FONT>for the quarter ended June 30, 2023</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 20px"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 20px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Total
cash of approximately&nbsp;$20.0 million at&nbsp;June 30, 2023</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>Registered Direct Offering</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 20px"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 20px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Registered Direct Offering at a price of $2.00, a premium of 82% to the TMC closing share price on
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                August 11, with expected gross proceeds of approximately $27 million based on existing commitments</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 20px"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 20px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>The Registered Direct Offering on significantly above-market standard terms is led by largest TMC shareholder
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ERAS Capital, strategic partner Allseas, and <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">several </FONT>institutional investors<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">.
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     Chairman and CEO Gerard Barron and CFO Craig Shesky along with several TMC board members also participated in the
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     transaction.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 20px"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 20px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">The
transaction includes warrant coverage of 50% (1 warrant for every 2 common shares purchased) with a warrant strike price of $3.00 per
share</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 20px"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 20px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Warrants contain a call provision which forces exercise if the 30-day volume weighted-average
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                price (&ldquo;VWAP&rdquo;) of TMC shares exceeds $6.50, as well as an anti-dilution mechanism in which the exercise price resets
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                lower if the Company were to issue equity below $2.00 per share</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 20px"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 20px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Two
institutional investors and their designees can elect to increase commitments in this transaction at the same terms upon written notice
to the Company on or before September 15 in an aggregate additional amount of $11 million, if the closing TMC share price on trading day
immediately prior to such notice is $3.00 per share or less</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Gerard Barron, TMC Chairman and CEO, commented: &ldquo;<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">Raising
capital in volatile markets is not an easy task. However, the size,</FONT> the <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">quality and the
value of our resource portfolio combined with the determination of our team to responsibly develop this resource have helped us attract
</FONT>a diverse range of shareholders <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">who recognize the significant upside of this asset. We are
grateful to</FONT> our director and largest shareholder, Andrei Karkar, through his family office ERAS Capital <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">and
to our offshore partner and shareholder, Allseas, for their unwavering support. We are also delighted to see several institutional investors
participate in this financing round.</FONT> I&rsquo;d <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">also </FONT>like to thank our <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">board
of directors and management for participating in this financing, demonstrating a show of faith in our future</FONT>.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"></FONT></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Craig Shesky, Chief Financial Officer of <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">The
Metals Company</FONT>, commented: &ldquo;In the current market, the vast majority of follow-on offerings are issued at discounts to the
current share price<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">, but we</FONT> believe <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">a</FONT> premium
<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">is warranted given that the asset we are developing is world-class, needle-moving and transformational.
This transaction is an important step on the path to unlocking the asset&rsquo;s true</FONT> value as we approach potential first production.&rdquo;</P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>Operational Highlights&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I></I></FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-decoration: double"><B>Corporate
                                            update on application timeline and costs, increased production capacity:</B></FONT> <FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">In
                                            August 2023, TMC provided a corporate update on expected <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">project
                                            </FONT>development timeline, production capacity and application costs for its NORI <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">Area
                                            </FONT>D Nodule Project following the recent International Seabed Authority (ISA) Council
                                            decisions on a roadmap to deliver final rules, regulations and procedures, also known as
                                            the Mining Code. TMC subsidiary Nauru Ocean Resources Inc. (NORI) intends to submit an application
                                            to the ISA for an exploitation contract for NORI Area D following the July 2024 meeting of
                                            the ISA. Assuming a one-year review process, NORI expects to be in commercial production
                                            in the fourth quarter of 2025 if the application is approved. NORI and strategic partner
                                            Allseas plan for an increased production capacity for the Project Zero Offshore System, using
                                            the Hidden Gem vessel, from an estimated 1.3 million wet tonnes to an estimated 3.0 million
                                            wet tonnes per annum, a potential increase of 130%.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I></I></FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-decoration: double"><B>Publication
                                            of NORI</B></FONT><B> <FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Data <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">to
                                            </FONT>Ocean Biodiversity Information System<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">:</FONT></FONT></B>
                                            <FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">In July 2023, TMC announced that
                                            data from two offshore environmental research campaigns conducted by NORI has been published
                                            by the <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">International Seabed Authority</FONT> to the
                                            Ocean Biodiversity Information System (OBIS), the world&rsquo;s largest scientific knowledge
                                            base on the diversity, distribution and abundance of marine organisms. NORI is now the single
                                            largest contributor of biological occurrence data to the OBIS ISA-node, providing approximately
                                            60% of all records. <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">With much more data to be submitted,
                                            we</FONT> expect NORI <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">Area </FONT>D will be one of
                                            the most highly-characterized <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">deep-sea </FONT>areas
                                            in <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">the</FONT> region that <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">hosts
                                            </FONT>approximately 90% <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">of </FONT>all nodule exploration.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I></I></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>Industry Update</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>International
                                            Seabed Authority<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">: </FONT></B>The ISA Council concluded
                                            Part II of its 28<SUP>th</SUP> Session in Kingston, Jamaica, where <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">there
                                            was a high level of motivation and </FONT>collaboration between Member States <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">who
                                            made significant</FONT> progress on the Mining Code <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">for
                                            commercial production</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">agreed by</FONT> consensus
                                            a roadmap to continue the elaboration of the Mining Code during formal sessions in November
                                            2023, March 2024 and July 2024 and informal intersessional working groups. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-decoration: double"><B>House
                                            leaders&rsquo; letter to Biden Administration and NDAA focus on nodules:</B></FONT> <FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">In
                                            July 2023, TMC welcomed a letter from U.S. Congressional leaders and several members of the
                                            U.S. House of Representatives Armed Services Committee urging the Biden Administration and
                                            the Department of Defense to assess domestic processing of seafloor polymetallic nodules
                                            as a means to secure key energy transition metals and &ldquo;close national security vulnerabilities.&rdquo;
                                            In June 2023, TMC welcomed the inclusion of polymetallic nodules in a report requested by
                                            the House Armed Services Committee to the Assistant Secretary of Defense for Industrial Base
                                            Policy under the National Defense Authorization Act (&ldquo;NDAA&rdquo;) which was passed
                                            by the House on July 14, 2023. Entitled &ldquo;H.R. 2670 &ndash; National Defense Authorization
                                            Act for Fiscal Year 2024; and H.R. 1282 &ndash; Major Richard Star Act&rdquo;<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: double">,
                                            </FONT>the U.S. House Armed Services request under the NDAA includes a &ldquo;roadmap recommending
                                            how the United States can have the ability to source and/or process critical minerals in
                                            innovative arenas, such as deep-sea mining, to decrease reliance on sources from foreign
                                            adversaries and bolster domestic competencies.&rdquo; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>Financial Results Overview</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B></B>At&nbsp;June
30, 2023, TMC held cash of&nbsp;$20.0 million&nbsp;and held no debt. We believe that our cash on hand, the expected net proceeds from
the registered direct offering and borrowing availability under our recently amended and extended credit facility with an affiliate of
Allseas will be sufficient to meet our working capital and capital expenditure commitments for at least the next twelve months from
today.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">TMC reported net loss of
approximately $14.1 million, or $0.05 per share for the quarter ended June 30, 2023, compared to net loss of $12.4 million, or $0.05
per share, for the quarter ended June 30, 2022. The net loss in Q2 2022 includes a credit of $5.7 million from the reduction in our
warrants liability, while Q2 2023 reflects a charge of $0.8 million for the increase in our warrants liability. Exploration
evaluation expenses during the quarter ended June 30, 2023 were $8.1 million compared to $10.2 million for the quarter ended June
30, 2022. General and administrative expenses were $5.1 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2023 compared to $8.1 million for the
quarter ended June 30, 2022. The lower spending in the second quarter of 2023 reflect lower share-based compensation, as options with
specific market capitalization vesting conditions were fully amortized in 2022, and lower spending on the PMTS as the collector test
was completed in November 2022, offset by an increase in prefeasibility study spending and an increase in mining, technological and
process development due to the engineering work which commenced in the fourth quarter of 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B></B></FONT><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>About&nbsp;The Metals Company</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">The Metals Company&nbsp;is an explorer
of lower-impact battery metals from seafloor polymetallic nodules, on a dual mission: (1) supply metals for the clean energy transition
with the least possible negative environmental and social impact and (2) accelerate the transition to a circular metal economy. The Company
through its subsidiaries holds exploration and commercial rights to three polymetallic nodule contract areas in the&nbsp;Clarion Clipperton
Zone&nbsp;of the&nbsp;Pacific Ocean&nbsp;regulated by the&nbsp;International Seabed Authority and sponsored by the governments of&nbsp;Nauru,&nbsp;Kiribati&nbsp;and
the Kingdom of&nbsp;Tonga. More information is available at&nbsp;<U>www.metals.co</U>.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>More info</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Media | media@metals.co</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Investors | investors@metals.co</P>

..report .reu td {
	border-bottom: 1px solid black;
}

	background-color: white;
}

	border-bottom: 1px solid black;
}

	border-bottom: 0px solid black;
}

	white-space: nowrap;
}

	text-align: right;
	white-space: nowrap;
}

	padding-left: 2em;
}

	padding: 0px 0.4em 0px 2em;
}

	text-align: left;
	white-space: normal;
}

}
